This store has been here as long as I can remember, hometown.  I haven't lived in SR for many years, but as an apartment dweller I sometimes do car maintenance when I come visit the folks and borrow a driveway.  Probably haven't quite done 50 oil changes (I don't believe in this new 'every 3500-4000mi' bs), yet I still too frequently forget to buy a new washer before a change (hey it's like a buck and if you've ever left a few drops of oil on someone else's driveway......not fun not cool).  Was in town hoping to find a washer quick, pre-Christmas/raging covid period, thinking/hoping this store was still there and could hook me up - they were and totally did, cheap!  Got like half dozen for under $5, nice. Guys were polite cordial/professional too.  But here's what triggered this review:  I drove by a empty covid looking parking lot broad daylight middle of the day.  Peak in the window and see workers, the door was open, sweet.  I go in there and there's like literally only ONE customer, and the guys behind the counter chattin like bros or good friends about something, reminding me of my younger years jobs.  But here's the kicker, they were all wearing masks!  With only one customer in the store!  idc if you're left or right or upside down middle - this is a real virus and people have really been DYING from it......  So props on you fellas working that day, and NAPA Auto Parts for a life saving policy and good quality employees, no wonder this store is still here.  Family owned/operated by chance??< /text>

<Review>My motto in life as is in Yelp is always under promise and over deliver so I apologize in advance if my review is too good to live up to but Tip's House is the best Thai joint I've ever had PERIOD.  So much so that if I was not so lazy, I would go subtract 1 star from all other Thai places I gave 5 stars to because this place is that much better than the rest, especially if you're comparing to Thai restaurants in or around Ktown to DTLA.  I'm talking about in terms of flavor, quality, freshness, portions, price, and customer service.  Yes, this place is that much better than the rest.

There's a reason why this little cute hole in the wall restaurant has been in business for 25+ years.  All the locals nearby know and swear by it.  If you've never been, give it a try!  If you've never had Thai food or if you're not well versed in Thai food, pick up the phone and the nice lady who's always there will help you.  People who run this place is super nice, kind, and patient.  (I say "people" but I've only dealt with this one lady who I presume to be the owner or maybe the daughter of the owner.)

Food is just unbelievably DELICIOUS!!!  Portions are VERY GENEROUS, especially for the price.  You get a good 1.5x more than most places.  Food is super fresh, made to order.  They are currently still serving during this COVID pandemic.  The two times I've been during the COVID situation, they had parking space available literally right in front of the restaurant and the nice lady brought my food out right away.  I mean for goodness sake, how many Thai places do you see pack hot sauce and picked jalapenos when you didn't even ask for them?!?!  This place really cares about their customers as they should!  (Restaurants like this has really disappeared and it's so unforunate!)

Shrimp Pad Thai is a must.  YES!!!  I was never a big Pad Thai fan but yes, this is a must.  Chicken Pad See Yew is bomb!  Panang Chicken curry is super delicious!  We tried the garlic beef today which was amazing.  (Beware: You will be blowing out garlic breath like a Dragon for the rest of the day if you get this garlic beef tho.)  All this for exactly $40.50!!!

My wife and I eat like the dinosaurs in Jurassic Park and we still have just as much food left over for dinner.  I keep forgetting to take pics because we're just so excited but I promise I'll post pics next time!<//Review><Response>None< /Response><Name>David Na</Name><rate>5< /rate>< date>

<UserId.>110497948134407292742< /UserId.><username>Chloe Horton</username><Date>1430663557147< /Date><rating>4< /rating>< text>
We're on our way home from work when we stopped by this place for early dinner. We just wanted to try Portuguese food and eating this type of food for the first time made us really excited. This place is small. When we came, there were only two tables left. We ordered two of their spicy dinner special. Although too spicy for us but the taste was great. I ordered myself a pad Thai and it was the best I have had. Very spicy but incredibly flavourful! We even ordered one more for my co-worker. Every one of us had a great time eating Portuguese food for the first time.

The downfall of this place are their parking area and the eating area. Both are small. So instead of five star, I will rate them 4.< /text>

< Text>
#7 BBQ pork spare rib & thai iced tea.

Those words don't even need to come out of my mouth, as I have been a repeat customer here for the last 13 years and they know me like family now. My mom has been coming here since 1991, and swears it hasn't changed a bit since. Tip's House has had exceptional food and service since the first time I walked through the glass door.

The dressing they use for the starter salad is unbelievable, causing me to buy a small container every time i pass by (They technically don't sell it to customers, but they know i travel far to visit them). The sauce they use for their BBQ is delicious as it doesn't over power the rich flavors of the spare rib. The egg rolls are probably the best I have ever had, perfectly crunchy, with the most balanced sweet & sour sauce to go along with it.

My mom and grandma swear by the spicy garlic shrimp which also looks like a mouth-watering delicacy of its own.

Needless to say, this is one place that I hope never changes, because it's not just the great food that makes Tip's House have an emotional connection with my past, but their attention and devotion to caring for customers is impeccable.</Text>

Chipotle is popular but it's only above average.
You don't get easy access to sauces and chips like most authentic Mexican places do.

The taste is ok but the food is barely spicy. You WILL need to add a lot of green tobasco sauce if you are used to spices.

I recommend Don Quixote over this place which is within a 1 mile radius from here.</review>
